style="text-align:center">\n<div style="text-align:left;margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto;"><ol style="list-style-type: lower-alpha; margin-left: 1em; font-size:90%;">\n<li value="1">The <a href="/wiki/First_language" title="First language">mother tongue</a> of Mauritians (2011 Census).<sup id="cite_ref-2011census_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2011census-5">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup></li>\n</ol></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>Mauritius</b> (<span class="nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="&#39;m&#39; in &#39;my&#39;">m</span><span title="/\xc9\x99/: &#39;a&#39; in &#39;about&#39;">\xc9\x99</span><span title="/\xcb\x88/: primary stress follows">\xcb\x88</span><span title="&#39;r&#39; in &#39;rye&#39;">r</span><span title="/\xc9\xaa/: &#39;i&#39; in &#39;kit&#39;">\xc9\xaa</span><span title="/\xca\x83/: &#39;sh&#39; in &#39;shy&#39;">\xca\x83</span></span>(<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/i/: &#39;y&#39; in &#39;happy&#39;">i</span></span>)<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/\xc9\x99/: &#39;a&#39; in &#39;about&#39;">\xc9\x99</span><span title="&#39;s&#39; in &#39;sigh&#39;">s</span></span>, <wbr /><span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="&#39;m&#39; in &#39;my&#39;">m</span><span title="/\xc9\x94\xcb\x90/: &#39;au&#39; in &#39;fraud&#39;">\xc9\x94\xcb\x90</span></span>-/</a></span><small class="nowrap">&#160;(<span class="unicode haudio"><span class="fn"><span style="white-space:nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:En-us-Mauritius.ogg" title="About this sound"><img alt="About this sound" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" width="11" height="11" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="20" data-file-height="20" /></a>&#160;</span><a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/a/a9/En-us-Mauritius.ogg" class="internal" title="En-us-Mauritius.ogg">listen</a></span></span>)</small></span>; <a href="/wiki/French_language" title="French language">French</a>: <i lang="fr">Maurice</i>), officially the <b>Republic of Mauritius</b> (French: <i lang="fr">R\xc3\xa9publique de Maurice</i>), is a <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">sovereign state</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Mascarene_Islands" title="Mascarene Islands">Mascarene archipelago</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Indian_Ocean" title="Indian Ocean">Indian Ocean</a>, located 2,000 kilometres (1,200&#160;mi) off the southeast coast of the <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">Africa</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_Mauritius" title="Constitution of Mauritius">constitution of Mauritius</a> declares the country\'s sovereignty over <a href="/wiki/Mauritius_Island" title="Mauritius Island">Mauritius Island</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rodrigues" title="Rodrigues">Rodrigues</a>, <a href="/wiki/Agal%C3%A9ga" title="Agal\xc3\xa9ga">Agal\xc3\xa9ga</a>, <a href="/wiki/St._Brandon" title="St. Brandon">St. Brandon</a> and the disputed territories of <a href="/wiki/Tromelin" class="mw-redirect" title="Tromelin">Tromelin</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Chagos_Archipelago" title="Chagos Archipelago">Chagos Archipelago</a>. The country\'s nearest neighbors include <a href="/wiki/Reunion" class="mw-disambig" title="Reunion">Reunion</a>, a French overseas department, and <a href="/wiki/Madagascar" title="Madagascar">Madagascar</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> The capital and largest city is <a href="/wiki/Port_Louis" title="Port Louis">Port Louis</a>. Other towns include <a href="/wiki/Quatre-Bornes" class="mw-redirect" title="Quatre-Bornes">Quatre-Bornes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Curepipe" title="Curepipe">Curepipe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vacoas-Phoenix" title="Vacoas-Phoenix">Vacoas-Phoenix</a> and <a href="/wiki/Beau_Bassin-Rose_Hill" title="Beau Bassin-Rose Hill">Beau Bassin-Rose Hill</a>\n</p><p>It is widely speculated that Mauritius was known to early <a href="/wiki/Phoenecian" class="mw-redirect" title="Phoenecian">Phoenecian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Arabs" title="Arabs">Arab</a> traders.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> After <a href="/wiki/Vasco_Da_Gama" class="mw-redirect" title="Vasco Da Gama">Vasco Da Gama</a> opened a new European shipping route to Asia, Mauritius was included in <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_people" title="Portuguese people">Portuguese</a> maps. The uninhabited island came under <a href="/wiki/Dutch_Mauritius" title="Dutch Mauritius">Dutch control</a> in the 16th century and was named after <a href="/wiki/Maurice,_Prince_of_Orange" title="Maurice, Prince of Orange">Maurice, Prince of Orange</a>. Mauritius was a French colony between 1715 and 1810, with the name <a href="/wiki/Isle_de_France" class="mw-redirect mw-disambig" title="Isle de France">Isle de France</a>. Under the French, the European elite built a <a href="/wiki/Plantation_economy" title="Plantation economy">plantation economy</a> with slaves imported from Africa. The <a href="/wiki/British_Empire" title="British Empire">British Empire</a> took control of the colony in 1810. The <a href="/wiki/Slavery_Abolition_Act_1833" title="Slavery Abolition Act 1833">abolition of slavery</a> was implemented in 1835. <a href="/wiki/British_Mauritius" title="British Mauritius">British Mauritius</a> was a <a href="/wiki/Crown_colony" title="Crown colony">crown colony</a> which received migrants from the <a href="/wiki/Indian_subcontinent" title="Indian subcontinent">Indian subcontinent</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Far_East" title="Far East">Far East</a>. <a href="/wiki/Seychelles" title="Seychelles">Seychelles</a> was separated from Mauritius in 1903. <a href="/wiki/Indentured_servitude" title="Indentured servitude">Indentured servitude</a> was ended in 1917.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> In 1948, an elected Legislature was established. In 1959, the first <a href="/wiki/Mauritian_general_election,_1959" title="Mauritian general election, 1959">election</a> based on <a href="/wiki/Universal_suffrage" title="Universal suffrage">universal suffrage</a> was held. Mauritius gained independence as a <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_dominion" class="mw-redirect" title="Commonwealth dominion">Commonwealth dominion</a> in 1968, with <a href="/wiki/Queen_Elizabeth" class="mw-disambig" title="Queen Elizabeth">Queen Elizabeth</a> as its last monarch represented by a <a href="/wiki/Governor_General_of_Mauritius" class="mw-redirect" title="Governor General of Mauritius">Governor General</a>. The country became a republic in 1992.  \n</p><p>Mauritius is a <a href="/wiki/Melting_pot" title="Melting pot">melting pot</a> with four major communities, including <a href="/wiki/Mauritian_of_Indian_origin" class="mw-redirect" title="Mauritian of Indian origin">Indo-Mauritians</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mauritian_of_French_origin" title="Mauritian of French origin">Franco-Mauritians</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mauritian_of_African_origin" title="Mauritian of African origin">Afro-Mauritians</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mauritian_of_Chinese_origin" class="mw-redirect" title="Mauritian of Chinese origin">Sino-Mauritians</a>. English continues to be the language of government, while <a href="/wiki/French_language" title="French language">French</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mauritian_Creole" title="Mauritian Creole">Mauritian Creole</a> are widely used for culture and daily life. The <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Mauritius" title="Economy of Mauritius">economy of Mauritius</a>, once dependent on <a href="/wiki/Sugar" title="Sugar">sugar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rum" title="Rum">rum</a> exports, has diversified into financial services, manufacturing, logistics and <a href="/wiki/Tourism_in_Mauritius" title="Tourism in Mauritius">tourism</a>. In 2018, Mauritius was ranked 49th in the <a href="/wiki/Global_Financial_Centres_Index" title="Global Financial Centres Index">Global Financial Centres Index</a>. The country is a <a href="/wiki/Parliamentary_republic" title="Parliamentary republic">parliamentary republic</a> modeled on the <a href="/wiki/Westminster_system" title="Westminster system">Westminster system</a>. The legal system has elements of both English and French law, including appeals to the <a href="/wiki/Privy_Council_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Privy Council of the United Kingdom">Privy Council</a> and influences from the <a href="/wiki/Napoleonic_Code" title="Napoleonic Code">Napoleonic Code</a>. Mauritius has the highest <a href="/wiki/Human_Development_Index" title="Human Development Index">Human Development Index</a> in Africa.  \n</p><p>As a trading nation, Mauritius gives priority to its relations with Western nations, <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> and China. It is a member of the <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth of Nations</a>, <a href="/wiki/La_Francophonie" class="mw-redirect" title="La Francophonie">La Francophonie</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Indian_Ocean_Commission" title="Indian Ocean Commission">Indian Ocean Commission</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Southern_African_Development_Community" title="Southern African Development Community">Southern African Development Community</a>, <a href="/wiki/COMESA" class="mw-redirect" title="COMESA">COMESA</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Indian_Ocean_Rim_Association" class="mw-redirect" title="Indian Ocean Rim Association">Indian Ocean Rim Association</a> and the <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Organization" title="World Trade Organization">World Trade Organization</a>.\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox"
